The `Makefile` provides the `gen-feature-toggles` target that runs the Go test twice to ensure feature flags are properly generated and validated.\\n\\nDocumentation in `contribute/feature-toggles.md` explains how to define new features and directs developers to update the CODEOWNERS file and use the registry-based codeowner system for feature ownership declaration.\\n\\nThis infrastructure ensures that code ownership is consistently enforced across multiple layers: GitHub's native CODEOWNERS validation, Go's type-safe feature management with codeowner integration, Kubernetes API resource definitions, and npm-based tools for parsing ownership information and routing quality issues to the appropriate teams.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3698,"cache_read_input_tokens":85998,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3698},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"16fcea20-8e78-49aa-a032-f79442083a15","uuid":"2218374e-cf4e-4e82-8e9d-da0b66ac7195"}
